%%\tagged{Ans@ShortAns, Type@Compute, Topic@Integral, Sub@Improper, Func@Rational, File@0069}{
\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Integration Compute Question 0069. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Determine if the integral converges or diverges.  If it converges, determine what it converges to.
\[
\int_{8}^\infty{{-\frac{4}{x^{4}}}\;dx}
\]

\input{Integral-Compute-0069.HELP.tex}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice{Diverges}
\choice[correct]{Converges}
\end{multipleChoice}

\begin{problem}
\[
\int_{8}^\infty{{-\frac{4}{x^{4}}}\;dx} = \answer{-\frac{1}{384}}
\]

\end{problem}

\end{problem}}%}

\begin{problem}

Determine if the integral converges or diverges.  If it converges, determine what it converges to.
\[
\int_{4}^\infty{{\frac{4}{x^{9}}}\;dx}
\]

\input{Integral-Compute-0069.HELP.tex}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice{Diverges}
\choice[correct]{Converges}
\end{multipleChoice}

\begin{problem}
\[
\int_{4}^\infty{{\frac{4}{x^{9}}}\;dx} = \answer{\frac{1}{131072}}
\]

\end{problem}

\end{problem}}%}

\choice{Diverges}
\choice[correct]{Converges}
\end{multipleChoice}

\begin{problem}
\[
\int_{1}^\infty{{\frac{1}{x^{2}}}\;dx} = \answer{1}
\]

\end{problem}

\end{problem}}%}

\int_{1}^\infty{{-\frac{3}{x^{8}}}\;dx}
\]

\input{Integral-Compute-0069.HELP.tex}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice{Diverges}
\choice[correct]{Converges}
\end{multipleChoice}

\begin{problem}
\[
\int_{1}^\infty{{-\frac{3}{x^{8}}}\;dx} = \answer{-\frac{3}{7}}
\]

\end{problem}

\end{problem}}%}

\[
\int_{6}^\infty{{\frac{2}{x^{3}}}\;dx}
\]

\input{Integral-Compute-0069.HELP.tex}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice{Diverges}
\choice[correct]{Converges}
\end{multipleChoice}

\begin{problem}
\[
\int_{6}^\infty{{\frac{2}{x^{3}}}\;dx} = \answer{\frac{1}{36}}
\]

\end{problem}

\end{problem}}%}

Determine if the integral converges or diverges.  If it converges, determine what it converges to.
\[
\int_{4}^\infty{{\frac{6}{x^{9}}}\;dx}
\]

\input{Integral-Compute-0069.HELP.tex}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice{Diverges}
\choice[correct]{Converges}
\end{multipleChoice}

\begin{problem}
\[
\int_{4}^\infty{{\frac{6}{x^{9}}}\;dx} = \answer{\frac{3}{262144}}
\]

\end{problem}

\end{problem}}%}

\int_{8}^\infty{{\frac{8}{x^{8}}}\;dx}
\]

\input{Integral-Compute-0069.HELP.tex}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice{Diverges}
\choice[correct]{Converges}
\end{multipleChoice}

\begin{problem}
\[
\int_{8}^\infty{{\frac{8}{x^{8}}}\;dx} = \answer{\frac{1}{1835008}}
\]

\end{problem}

\end{problem}}%}

\begin{problem}
\[
\int_{1}^\infty{{\frac{7}{x^{7}}}\;dx} = \answer{\frac{7}{6}}
\]

\end{problem}

\end{problem}}%}

\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Integration Compute Question 0069. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Determine if the integral converges or diverges.  If it converges, determine what it converges to.
\[
\int_{3}^\infty{{-\frac{4}{x}}\;dx}
\]

\input{Integral-Compute-0069.HELP.tex}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice{Diverges}
\choice[correct]{Converges}
\end{multipleChoice}

\begin{problem}
\[
\int_{3}^\infty{{-\frac{4}{x}}\;dx} = \answer{-\infty}
\]

\end{problem}

\end{problem}}%}
